Products and Capacity : Ketonic Resin (250 MTPM), M.F.Resin (20 MTPM), Water Base Adhesive (50 MTPM), PVB (Poly Vinyl Butryl Resin) (50 MTPM), Adhesion Promoter TA-10 (20 MTPM)
Project Details : Tridev Resins India is taking up an expansion project at its synthetic organic chemicals manufacturing unit, Vapi. The project involves the capacity addition of Ketonic Resin, M.F.Resin, Water Base Adhesive, PVB (Poly Vinyl Butryl Resin) and Adhesion Promoter TA-10 and for which Cyclohexanone, Melamine, Butyl acrylate, etc are the raw materials used. As of February 2015, company has approached MoEF for clearances.
